data-bm="11"><h2><a href="https://www.solvusoft.com/en/file-extensions/file-extension-md/" h="ID=SERP,5167.1">MD File Extension: What Is It &amp; How To Open It?</a></h2><div class="b_caption"><div class="b_attribution" u="2|5061|4644004037527762|3FQ3n00Lcrg_2XNTzQUxoQ0096wTxUsB"><cite>https://<strong>www.solvusoft.com</strong>/en/<strong>file</strong>-extensions/<strong>file-extension-md</strong></cite><a href="#" aria-label="Actions for this site" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false" role="button"><span class="c_tlbxTrg"><span class="c_tlbxTrgIcn sw_ddgn"></span><span class="c_tlbxH" h="BASE:CACHEDPAGEDEFAULT" k="SERP,5168.1"></span></span></a></div><p><strong>MD File</strong> Summary. Our most recent information indicates that <strong>MD files</strong> are associated with seven unique <strong>file</strong> types (the most prevalent being the Markdown Documentation <strong>File</strong> format) and can be viewed primarily with Microsoft Notepad, including sixteen other known software applications (listed below).</p></div><div class="qbrs_data" data-appns="SERP" data-k="5362"></div></li><li class="b_algo" data-bm="12"><h2><a href="https://www.openthefile.net/file-extension/md" h="ID=SERP,5188.1">MD File Extension - What is a md file and how do I open a md file ...</a></h2><div class="b_caption"><div class="b_attribution" u="3|5062|5028412118468408|gAXD0UEtC67uqGUcyiNDHV6RnWLXsnFf"><cite>https://www.<strong>open</strong>the<strong>file</strong>.net/<strong>file</strong>-extension/<strong>md</strong></cite><a href="#" aria-label="Actions for this site" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false" role="button"><span class="c_tlbxTrg"><span class="c_tlbxTrgIcn sw_ddgn"></span><span class="c_tlbxH" h="BASE:CACHEDPAGEDEFAULT" k="SERP,5189.1"></span></span></a></div><p>What is a <strong>md file</strong> and how do I <strong>open</strong> a <strong>md file</strong>? These are text <strong>files</strong> used as Markdown Documentation <strong>Files</strong> through Markdown language dialects. <strong>MD files</strong> are usually saved in plain text format including inline text symbols, defining how a text is formatted such as the indentations, its table formatting, fonts, and headers.</p><div class="b_factrow b_twofr"><div class="b_vlist2col"><ul><li><div class="b_sritem b_srtxtstarcolor">4/5<span class="csrc sc_rc1" role="img" aria-label="Star Rating: 4 out of 5." data-tag="item.customratingitem"><span class="sw_st"></span><span class="sw_st"></span><span class="sw_st"></span><span class="sw_st"></span><span class="sw_ste"></span></span><div class="b_sritemp">(2)</div></div></li></ul><ul></ul></div></div></div><div class="qbrs_data" data-appns="SERP" data-k="5366"></div></li><li class="b_ans b_mop b_mopb" data-bm="13"><div class="b_vPanel"><div><div class="FEDescTitle">MD file extension</div></div><div>An MD file is a text file created using one of several possible dialects of the Markdown language.  It is saved in plain text format but includes inline text symbols that define how to format the text (e.g., bold, indentations, headers, table formatting).  MD files are designed for authoring plain text documentation that can be easily converted to HTML.</div><div><div id="feFooter"><span class="b_footnote">Data from: <a href="https://fileinfo.com/extension/md" h="ID=SERP,5369.1">fileinfo.com</a></span></div></div></div></li><li class="b_ans b_mop b_mopb" data-bm="14"><div class="b_sideBleed b_topBleed
